firewall {
    family inet {
        filter PROTECT-RE {
            term fragment-first {
                from {
                    first-fragment;
                }
                then {
                    count DDOS-FRAGMENT;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term fragment-is {
                from {
                    is-fragment;
                }
                then {
                    count DDOS-FRAGMENT;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term SMALL-PACKETS {
                from {
                    packet-length 0-24;
                }
                then {
                    count SMALL-PACKET-ATTACK;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term TCP-DOS-PROTECTION {
                from {
                    /* all incoming TCP based sessions i.e. only SYN */
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP-ADDRESSES;
                        LOCALHOST;
                        MGMT-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    tcp-flags "(syn & !ack) | fin | rst";
                }
                then {
                    policer TCP-CONNECTION-POLICER;
                    count TCP-SYN;
                    next term;
                }
            }
            term BFD {
                from {
                    protocol udp;
                    port [ 3784 3785 4784 6784 ];
                }
                then {
                    count BFD-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term SSH-IN {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        SSH-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    port ssh;
                }
                then {
                    policer SSH-POLICER;
                    count SSH-IN-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term BGP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP-ADDRESSES;
                        BGP-ADDRESSES-RI;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    port bgp;
                }
                then {
                    count BGP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term SNMP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        PR-SNMP-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    destination-port snmp;
                }
                then {
                    policer SNMP-POLICER;
                    count SNMP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term NTP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        NTP-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    port ntp;
                }
                then {
                    policer NTP-POLICER;
                    count NTP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term ISP-LINK-PING {
                from {
                    prefix-list {
                        ISP-LINK-PING-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol icmp;
                    icmp-type-except [ router-advertisement redirect ];
                }
                then {
                    inactive: policer ISP-LINK-PING-POLICER;
                    count ISP-LINK-PING-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term ICMP {
                from {
                    protocol icmp;
                    icmp-type-except [ router-advertisement redirect ];
                }
                then {
                    inactive: policer ICMP-POLICER;
                    count ICMP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term tacacs {
                from {
                    address {
                        84.235.0.34/32;
                        10.171.1.251/32;
                        10.141.48.110/32;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    source-port tacacs;
                    tcp-established;
                }
                then {
                    count tacacs-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term MPLS-ECHO-REPLY {
                from {
                    destination-prefix-list {
                        MPLS-INFRASTRUCTURE;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    source-port 3503;
                }
                then {
                    count MPLS-ECHO-REPLY;
                    accept;
                }
            }

                }

                }
            }
            term RSVP {

                    source-prefix-list {
                        MPLS-INFRASTRUCTURE;
                    }
                    protocol rsvp;
                }
                then {
                    count RSVP-TRAFFIC;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term LDP {

                    source-address {

                        84.235.111.0/24;
                    }
                    source-prefix-list {
                        MPLS-INFRASTRUCTURE;
                    }
                    protocol [ tcp udp ];
                    port ldp;
                }
                then accept;
            }
            term PCEP {

                        10.188.194.64/28;

                    port 4189;
                }

                        MGMT-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol udp;
                    source-port 1024-65535;
                }

                    count DENY-TO-ROUTING-ENGINE;
                    syslog;
                    discard;
                }
            }
        }
        filter FF_VPN_VIVA_KUWAIT {
            physical-interface-filter;
            term VIVA_KUWAIT_PREMIUM-DATA {
                from {
                    source-address {
                        94.128.2.0/28;
                        94.128.2.192/27;

                    forwarding-class PREMIUM-DATA;
                    force-premium;
                    next term;
                }
            }
            term default-all {
                then accept;
            }
            term VIVA_KUWAIT_S6a {

                }

            }
        }
        filter STC-TO-VIVA-KUWAIT {
            term S6a {
                from {
                    source-address {
                        212.215.134.14/32;
                        212.215.134.30/32;

        filter PROTECT-RE-IPv6 {
            term icmp {
                from {
                    next-header icmpv6;
                    icmp-type [ echo-request echo-reply destination-unreachable time-exceeded neighbor-solicit neighbor-advertisement ];
                }
                then {
                    policer SMALL-BW-POLICER;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term trace-route {
                from {
                    next-header udp;
                    destination-port 33434-33523;
                }
                then {
                    policer SMALL-BW-POLICER;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term tcp-connection {
                from {
                    next-header tcp;
                    tcp-flags "(syn & !ack) | fin | rst";
                }
                then {
                    policer TCP-CONNECTION-POLICER;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term BGP {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    next-header tcp;
                    port bgp;
                }
                then {
                    count BGP-TRAFFIC-IPv6;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term everything-else {
                then {
                    count denied-counter-IPv6;
                    discard;
                }
            }
        }

                    destination-prefix-list {
                        IPV6_REMOTE_ACCESS;
                    }
                    next-header icmp6;
                }
                then {
                    count PERMIT_VALID_ICMP_LOCAL;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term REJECT_INVALID_ICMP {
                from {
                    next-header icmpv6;
                    icmp-type [ neighbor-advertisement neighbor-solicit router-solicit router-advertisement redirect ];
                }
                then {
                    count REJECT_INVALID_ICMP;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term PERMIT_ALL {
                then accept;
            }
        }

        if-exceeding {

    }
    policer SMALL-BW-POLICER {

        }
        then discard;
    }

    }

            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }

        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 100m;
            burst-size-limit 62k;
        }
        then discard;

    policer POLICER_VPN_VIVA_KUWAIT_S6a {
        logical-bandwidth-policer;

            bandwidth-limit 2m;
            burst-size-limit 4k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer ARP-Policer {
        logical-interface-policer;
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 64k;
            burst-size-limit 1500;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    hierarchical-policer VPN_VIVA_KUWAIT_10G {
        aggregate {
            if-exceeding {
                bandwidth-limit 10g;
                burst-size-limit 6m;
            }
            then {
                discard;
            }
        }
        premium {
            if-exceeding {
                bandwidth-limit 102m;
                burst-size-limit 63k;
            }
            then {
                discard;
            }
        }
    }
